      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Frequent_flyer_programme">
        Frequent flyer programme
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Aeroflot&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Frequent flyer programme">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <table class="plainlinks metadata ambox ambox-content ambox-Advert" role="presentation">
       <tr>
        <td class="mbox-image">
         <div style="width:52px">
          <img alt="" data-file-height="40" data-file-width="40" height="40" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Ambox_important.svg/40px-Ambox_important.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Ambox_important.svg/60px-Ambox_important.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Ambox_important.svg/80px-Ambox_important.svg.png 2x" width="40"/>
         </div>
        </td>
        <td class="mbox-text">
         <div class="mbox-text-span">
          This article
          <b>
           contains content that is written like
           <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:What_Wikipedia_is_not#Wikipedia_is_not_a_soapbox_or_means_of_promotion" title="Wikipedia:What Wikipedia is not">
            an advertisement
           </a>
          </b>
          .
          <span class="hide-when-compact">
           Please help
           <a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Aeroflot&amp;action=edit">
            improve it
           </a>
           by removing
           <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Spam" title="Wikipedia:Spam">
            promotional content
           </a>
           and inappropriate
           <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:External_links" title="Wikipedia:External links">
            external links
           </a>
           , and by adding encyclopedic content written from a
           <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Neutral_point_of_view" title="Wikipedia:Neutral point of view">
            neutral point of view
           </a>
           .
          </span>
          <small>
           <i>
            (February 2018)
           </i>
          </small>
          <small class="hide-when-compact">
           <i>
            (
            <a href="/wiki/Help:Maintenance_template_removal" title="Help:Maintenance template removal">
             Learn how and when to remove this template message
            </a>
            )
           </i>
          </small>
         </div>
        </td>
       </tr>
      </table>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Aeroflot_Bonus_logo.png">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="69" data-file-width="286" height="53" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/5/58/Aeroflot_Bonus_logo.png/220px-Aeroflot_Bonus_logo.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/5/58/Aeroflot_Bonus_logo.png 1.5x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Aeroflot_Bonus_logo.png" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         Aeroflot Bonus logo
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       Aeroflot uses Aeroflot Bonus as their
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Frequent-flyer_programme" title="Frequent-flyer programme">
        frequent-flyer programme
       </a>
       . It has three levels:
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-164">
        <a href="#cite_note-164">
         [163]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <center>
       <table class="wikitable">
        <caption>
         <b>
          Aeroflot Bonus Levels
         </b>
        </caption>
        <tr>
         <th>
          Level
         </th>
         <th>
          Benefits
         </th>
         <th>
          Requirements
         </th>
         <th>
          <a href="/wiki/SkyTeam" title="SkyTeam">
           SkyTeam
          </a>
          Status
         </th>
        </tr>
        <tr>
         <td style="background:#4169e1; text-align:center;">
          Regular
         </td>
         <td align="left">
          <ul>
           <li>
            No benefits on Regular Level
           </li>
          </ul>
         </td>
         <td>
          Travelers can start their participation in Aeroflot Bonus Programme from the age of 2 (Aeroflot Junior)
         </td>
         <td>
          –
         </td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
         <td style="background:silver; text-align:center;">
          Silver
         </td>
         <td align="left">
          <ul>
           <li>
            Tier Bonus Miles – 25% of the flown distance
           </li>
           <li>
            Preferred Seating
           </li>
           <li>
            Priority Check-In
           </li>
           <li>
            Extra 10 kg baggage allowance or 1 piece on routes where piece concept systems is applicable (Only on Aeroflot regular flights)
           </li>
           <li>
            Boarding with first and business class passengers
           </li>
           <li>
            Priority reservation waitlisting
           </li>
          </ul>
         </td>
         <td>
          25,000 miles (40,000 km) or
          <br/>
          25 flight segments during calendar year
         </td>
         <td>
          <a href="/wiki/SkyTeam#SkyTeam_Elite" title="SkyTeam">
           Elite
          </a>
         </td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
         <td style="background:Goldenrod; text-align:center;">
          Gold
         </td>
         <td align="left">
          <ul>
           <li>
            Tier Bonus Miles – 50% of the flown distance
           </li>
           <li>
            Priority Check-In
           </li>
           <li>
            The opportunity "Comfort +" is given free of charge
            <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-165">
             <a href="#cite_note-165">
              [164]
             </a>
            </sup>
           </li>
           <li>
            Extra 20 kg baggage allowance or 2 piece on routes where piece concept systems is applicable (Only on Aeroflot regular flights)
           </li>
           <li>
            Preferred Seating
           </li>
           <li>
            Lounge Access
           </li>
           <li>
            Invite a traveling companion to Business Class lounges
           </li>
           <li>
            Priority Airport Standby
           </li>
           <li>
            High priority waitlisting (above Silver)
           </li>
           <li>
            Boarding with first and business class passengers
           </li>
           <li>
            Priority Baggage Handling
           </li>
          </ul>
         </td>
         <td>
          50,000 miles (80,000 km) or
          <br/>
          50 flight segments during calendar year
         </td>
         <td>
          <a href="/wiki/SkyTeam#SkyTeam_Elite_Plus" title="SkyTeam">
           Elite Plus
          </a>
         </td>
        </tr>
       </table>
      </center>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Sponsorship_and_promotion_agreements">
        Sponsorship and promotion agreements
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Aeroflot&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Sponsorship and promotion agreements">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <p>
       As of July 2013
       <sup class="plainlinks noexcerpt noprint asof-tag update" style="display:none;">
        <a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Aeroflot&amp;action=edit">
         [update]
        </a>
       </sup>
       , Aeroflot is the official carrier of
       <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C." title="Manchester United F.C.">
        Manchester United
       </a>
       .
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Aeroflot_come_on_board_166-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-Aeroflot_come_on_board-166">
         [165]
        </a>
       </sup>
       The agreement is the first ever sponsorship Manchester United has signed with a Russian company.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Manchester_United_makes_Aeroflot_its_first_Russian_sponsor_167-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-Manchester_United_makes_Aeroflot_its_first_Russian_sponsor-167">
         [166]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>

           <a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20150902110459/http://atwonline.com/finance-data/russia-s-aeroflot-acquire-transaero-airlines" rel="nofollow">
            "Russia's Aeroflot to acquire Transaero Airlines"
           </a>
           .
           <a href="/wiki/Air_Transport_World" title="Air Transport World">
            Air Transport World
           </a>
           . Archived from
           <a class="external text" href="http://atwonline.com/finance-data/russia-s-aeroflot-acquire-transaero-airlines" rel="nofollow">
            the original
           </a>
           on 2 September 2015.
           <q>
            Russia’s largest airline, Aeroflot, will acquire
            <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Transaero_Airlines" title="Transaero Airlines">
             Transaero Airlines
            </a>
            , according to a Transaero statement.
           </q>
          </cite>

         <span class="reference-text">

           <q>
            Russia's llyushin Il-86 widebody has entered scheduled service with Aeroflot. Shown here is an Il-86 after a two-hour route-proving flight between Moscow and Mineralnye Vody. First scheduled route for the type is between Moscow's Vnukovo Airport and Tashkent, operated three times a week.
           </q>

         <span class="mw-cite-backlink">
          <b>
           <a href="#cite_ref-Other_News_–_01/14/2010_126-0">
            ^
           </a>
          </b>
         </span>
         <span class="reference-text">
          <cite class="citation news">
           <a class="external text" href="https://www.webcitation.org/698az5aol?url=http://atwonline.com/aircraft-engines-components/news/other-news-01142010-0114" rel="nofollow">
            "Other News – 01/14/2010"
           </a>
           .
           <a href="/wiki/Air_Transport_World" title="Air Transport World">
            Air Transport World
           </a>
           . 15 January 2010. Archived from
           <a class="external text" href="http://atwonline.com/aircraft-engines-components/news/other-news-01142010-0114" rel="nofollow">
            the original
           </a>
           on 13 July 2012
           <span class="reference-accessdate">
            . Retrieved
            <span class="nowrap">
             13 July
            </span>
            2012
           </span>
           .
           <q>
            Aeroflot announced the retirement of its last Tu-154. The aircraft flew for the final time on December 31 from Yekaterinburg to Moscow Sheremetyevo, according to
            <a href="/wiki/RIA_Novosti" title="RIA Novosti">
             RIA Novosti
            </a>
            , and will be replaced with an A320.

           <a class="external text" href="https://www.webcitation.org/6HzAWqI9r?url=http://www.reuters.com/article/2013/07/08/us-manchester-united-aeroflot-idUSBRE9670EW20130708" rel="nofollow">
            Archived
           </a>
           from the original on 9 July 2013.
          </cite>
          <span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Ajournal&amp;rft.genre=article&amp;rft.atitle=Manchester+United+makes+Aeroflot+its+first+Russian+sponsor&amp;rft.date=2013-07-08&amp;rft.aulast=Weir&amp;rft.aufirst=Keith&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.reuters.com%2Farticle%2F2013%2F07%2F08%2Fus-manchester-united-aeroflot-idUSBRE9670EW20130708&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AAeroflot">
           <span style="display:none;">
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </li>
       </ol>
